<div id="videocontainer" style="padding-bottom:10px;margin: 0 auto;min-width: 400px;width: 50vh;max-width: 700px;"></div><h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of Pokémon by Hoenn Pokédex number (Generation III)</h1><div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content"><div id="siteSub">From Bulbapedia, the community-driven Pokémon encyclopedia.</div><div id="contentSub" lang="en" dir="ltr"></div><div id="jump-to-nav"></div><a href="#column-one" class="mw-jump-link">Jump to navigation</a><a href="#searchInput" class="mw-jump-link">Jump to search</a><div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:162px;"><a href="/wiki/File:RSE_Pok%C3%A9dex.png" class="image"><img alt src="//archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/d/d1/RSE_Pok%C3%A9dex.png/160px-RSE_Pok%C3%A9dex.png" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="160" height="184" class="thumbimage" srcset="//archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/d/d1/RSE_Pok%C3%A9dex.png/240px-RSE_Pok%C3%A9dex.png 1.5x, //archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/d/d1/RSE_Pok%C3%A9dex.png/320px-RSE_Pok%C3%A9dex.png 2x" /></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:RSE_Pok%C3%A9dex.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Hoenn" title="Hoenn">Hoenn</a> region's Pokédex (Generation III)</div></div></div>
<p>This is a list of Pokémon in the order dictated by the <a href="/wiki/Hoenn" title="Hoenn">Hoenn</a> <a href="/wiki/Regional_Pok%C3%A9dex" title="Regional Pokédex">regional Pokédex</a>, meaning that the <a href="/wiki/Starter_Pok%C3%A9mon#Hoenn" title="Starter Pokémon">starter Pokémon from Hoenn</a> will appear first, followed by Pokémon native to the Hoenn region.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Generation_I" title="Generation I">Generation I</a> and <a href="/wiki/Generation_II" title="Generation II">II</a> Pokémon not native to the Hoenn region also have a Hoenn Pokédex number greater than 202; these numbers are not usually displayed by either the game or official sources.
</p><p>When viewing this listing in <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Bank" title="Pokémon Bank">Pokémon Bank</a>, it is labeled "Good Old Hoenn".
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="In_the_spin-off_games">In the spin-off games</span></h2>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9dex_(Pinball)" title="Pokédex (Pinball)">Pokédex</a> in <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Pinball:_Ruby_%26_Sapphire" title="Pokémon Pinball: Ruby &amp; Sapphire">Pokémon Pinball: Ruby &amp; Sapphire</a> displays Pokémon organized by the Generation III Hoenn Pokédex order, except <a href="/wiki/Deoxys_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Deoxys (Pokémon)">Deoxys</a> is unavailable in this game. After <a href="/wiki/Jirachi_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Jirachi (Pokémon)">Jirachi</a> (#385), there are 4 additional unnumbered Pokémon, listed in this order: <a href="/wiki/Chikorita_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Chikorita (Pokémon)">Chikorita</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cyndaquil_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Cyndaquil (Pokémon)">Cyndaquil</a>, <a href="/wiki/Totodile_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Totodile (Pokémon)">Totodile</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Aerodactyl_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Aerodactyl (Pokémon)">Aerodactyl</a>.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span></h2>
<ul><li>Excluding unseen numbers, the Hoenn Pokédex in Generations III and VI is the only one not to include the <a href="/wiki/Eevee_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Eevee (Pokémon)">Eevee</a> evolutionary family.</li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Ruby_and_Sapphire_Versions" title="Pokémon Ruby and Sapphire Versions">Pokémon Ruby, Sapphire</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Emerald_Version" title="Pokémon Emerald Version">Emerald</a>:
<ul><li>If a player without the <a href="/wiki/National_Pok%C3%A9dex" title="National Pokédex">National Pokédex</a> owns a Pokémon not native to <a href="/wiki/Hoenn" title="Hoenn">Hoenn</a> (by trading with <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Colosseum" title="Pokémon Colosseum">Pokémon Colosseum</a>), that Pokémon will not appear in the Pokédex and it will not have a Pokédex number in the <a href="/wiki/Summary" title="Summary">summary</a> screen until the National Pokédex is obtained.</li>
<li>If a player catches a <a href="/wiki/Wild_Pok%C3%A9mon" title="Wild Pokémon">wild Pokémon</a> not native to <a href="/wiki/Hoenn" title="Hoenn">Hoenn</a> prior to obtaining the <a href="/wiki/National_Pok%C3%A9dex" title="National Pokédex">National Pokédex</a> (which is not possible in normal gameplay) and the player had not obtained that species before, the respective <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9dex" title="Pokédex">Pokédex</a> entry appears normally at the end of the battle (even though this entry remains inaccessible in the Pokédex itself). This entry seen at the end of battle includes the Hoenn Pokédex number that would normally be unseen (such as #203 for <a href="/wiki/Bulbasaur_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Bulbasaur (Pokémon)">Bulbasaur</a>).</li></ul></li></ul>

<script>
// Initialize elements
appendElementIf({id: "adthrive-left-s", wAbove: 1520, wBelow: 1699, hAbove: 700});
appendElementIf({id: "adthrive-left-m", wAbove: 1700, wBelow: 1890, hAbove: 700});
appendElementIf({id: "adthrive-left-l", wAbove: 1891, hAbove: 700});

appendElementIf({id: "adthrive-right-s", wAbove: 945, wBelow: 1099, hAbove: 964});
appendElementIf({id: "adthrive-right-m", wAbove: 1100, wBelow: 1399, hAbove: 964});
appendElementIf({id: "adthrive-right-l", wAbove: 1400, hAbove: 964});
appendElementIf({id: "adthrive-right-rect", hBelow: 964});


// Appends element if condition is met
function appendElementIf({id, wAbove, wBelow, hAbove, hBelow}) {

	// find browser height
	var w = window.innerWidth;
	var h = window.innerHeight;

	// If true after browser size check then unit is added
	var condition = true;

	// Check size conditions
	if (wBelow && (w > wBelow)) condition = false;
	if (wAbove && (w < wAbove)) condition = false;

	if (hBelow && (h > hBelow)) condition = false;
	if (hAbove && (h < hAbove)) condition = false;

	// Append element if condition is met
	if (condition) {
		createAndAppendElement(id);
	}
}


// creates and appends a div element to the body
function createAndAppendElement(id)
{
	var atEl = document.createElement('div');
	atEl.id = id;
	document.body.appendChild(atEl);
}
</script>


 <style>
        /*This styles are to place the close button right above the video without this the close button will be placed below the video.*/
        #pw-close-btn {
            display: none !important;
        }
        #span_btn {
            position: absolute;
            top: -40px;
            right: 0;
            cursor: pointer;
        }
        @media only screen and (max-width: 767px) {
            #span_btn {
                top: 9px;
                right: 11px;
            }
        }
        .is-docked {
           margin-bottom:90px !important;
        }
        </style>
